0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;"> &#8211; HealthEquity, Inc. (NASDAQ&#58; HQY) (&#34;HealthEquity&#34; or the &#34;Company&#34;), the nation's largest health savings account (&#34;HSA&#34;) non-bank custodian, today announced financial results for its first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2020, compared to its prior quarter ended April&#160;30, 2019, which did not include the acquisition of WageWorks.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8220;The team&#8217;s remarkable response to the COVID-19 pandemic has strengthened HealthEquity&#8217;s culture and accelerated promised synergies,&#8221; said Jon Kessler, President and CEO. &#8220;During a tumultuous quarter, 17% year-over-year increase in new HSA openings and 33% Adjusted EBITDA margin show just how deeply growth and profitability are embedded in our model.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">First quarter financial results</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Revenue for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2020 of $190.0&#160;million grew 118% compared to $87.1&#160;million for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2019. Revenue this quarter included&#58; service revenue of $111.3&#160;million, custodial revenue of $46.9&#160;million, and interchange revenue of $31.8&#160;million. </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity reported net income of $1.8&#160;million, or $0.03 per diluted share, and non-GAAP net income of $30.8&#160;million, or $0.43 per diluted share, for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2020. The Company reported net income of $41.8&#160;million, or $0.65 per diluted share, and non-GAAP net income of $27.4&#160;million, or $0.43 per diluted share, for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2019.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Adjusted EBITDA was $63.0&#160;million for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2020, an increase of 62% compared to $38.9&#160;million for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2019. Adjusted EBITDA was 33% of revenue compared to 45% for the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2019.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Account and asset metrics</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HSAs as of April&#160;30, 2020 were approximately 5.4&#160;million, an increase of 33% year over year, including 245,000 HSAs with investments, an increase of 38% year over year. Total Accounts as of April&#160;30, 2020 reached 12.7&#160;million, including 7.3&#160;million consumer-directed benefit (&#34;CDB&#34;) accounts.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Total HSA Assets as of April&#160;30, 2020 were $11.5&#160;billion, an increase of 38% year over year. Total HSA assets included $8.7&#160;billion of HSA cash and $2.8&#160;billion of HSA investments. Client-held funds, which are deposits held on behalf of our Clients to facilitate administration of our CDBs, and from which we generate custodial revenue, were $0.9&#160;billion as of April&#160;30, 2020.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">New HSA openings and HSA asset balances</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity reported sales of 104,000 new HSAs in the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2020, 17% more than in the first quarter ended April&#160;30, 2019. HSA members grew their cash balances by approximately $40.0&#160;million during the quarter, while total member balances decreased by approximately $37.0&#160;million due to the impact of market declines on invested balances, partially offset by net contributions from cash balances to investments.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">WageWorks integration</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity completed its acquisition of WageWorks on August 30, 2019. &#160;The Company accelerated its integration efforts and now expects to achieve the previously stated goal of $50 million in run rate synergies, including the on-shoring of all telephone-based member services to the United States, by the end of this year's fiscal second quarter ending July 31, 2020.</font></div><div style="position:relative;width:100%;height:54pt;"><div style="position:absolute;bottom:0;width:100%;"><div style="text-align:center;-sec-extract:summary;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">1</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="height:54pt;width:100%;"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Business outlook</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Due to uncertainty regarding the pace of reopening during the COVID-19 pandemic, the Company is withdrawing its full-year fiscal 2021 guidance. For the fiscal second quarter ending July 31, 2020, management expects revenues of $168 million to $173 million. Its outlook for net loss is between $20 million and $15 million, resulting in net loss per diluted share of $0.27 to $0.21. Its outlook for non-GAAP net income, calculated using the method described below, is between $17 million and $22 million, resulting in non-GAAP net income per diluted share of $0.23 to $0.30 (based on an estimated 73 million weighted-average shares outstanding). Management expects Adjusted EBITDA of $42 million to $48 million.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Said Kessler, &#8220;We believe the COVID-19 pandemic&#8217;s negative effect on our operating performance will fade as businesses gradually reopen, while the unprecedented economic fallout drives HSA growth and accelerates long-term trends favoring established market leaders like HealthEquity.&#8221;</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">See &#8220;Non-GAAP financial information&#8221; below for definitions of our Adjusted EBITDA and non-GAAP net income. A reconciliation of the non-GAAP financial measures used throughout this release to the most comparable GAAP financial measures is included with the financial tables at the end of this release.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Conference call</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">HealthEquity management will host a conference call at 4&#58;30 pm (Eastern Time) on Tuesday, June 2, 2020 to discuss the first quarter 2021 financial results. The conference call will be accessible by dialing 844-791-6252, or 661-378-9636 for international callers, and referencing conference ID 8297634. A live audio webcast of the call will also be available on the investor relations section of our website at http&#58;&#47;&#47;ir.healthequity.com.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;">Non-GAAP financial information </font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">To supplement our financial information presented on a GAAP basis, we disclose non-GAAP financial measures, including Adjusted EBITDA, non-GAAP net income, and non-GAAP net income per diluted share. </font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:36pt;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;">Adjusted EBITDA is adjusted earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization, amortization of acquired intangible assets, stock-based compensation expense, merger integration and acquisition-related costs, gains and losses on marketable equity securities, and other certain non-operating items. </font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:36pt;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;">Non-GAAP net income is calculated by adding back to net income before provision for income taxes the following items&#58; amortization of acquired intangible assets, stock-based compensation expense, merger integration and acquisition-related costs, and gains and losses on marketable equity securities.</font></div><div style="text-indent:-18pt;padding-left:36pt;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.5pt;">Non-GAAP net income per diluted share is calculated by dividing non-GAAP net income by diluted weighted-average shares outstanding.</font></div><div style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;"><font style="background-color:rgb(255,255,255, 0.0);color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;">Non-GAAP financial measures should be considered in addition to results prepared in accordance with GAAP and should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, GAAP results.
